;; Pathfinding using a simple graph
;; Graph is represented as facts: (= (edge A B) True) means there''s an one-way edge from A to B.
!(pragma! compile full)

    -->(0,'&self',['pragma!',compile,full],depth(0))
    <--(0,retval('Empty'))
      -->(0,'&self','Empty',depth(1))
; Evaluation took 0.359 ms. (358.60 microseconds) 
Deterministic: Empty

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',:,edge,[[->,'Symbol','Symbol','Bool']])
(: edge 
  (-> Symbol Symbol Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',=,[edge,a,b],'True')
(= 
  (edge a b) True)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',=,[edge,b,c],'True')
(= 
  (edge b c) True)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',=,[edge,c,d],'True')
(= 
  (edge c d) True)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',=,[edge,e,f],'True')
(= 
  (edge e f) True)


;;a -> b -> c -> d
;;     \
;;      e -> f
;; Pathfinding rule
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',:,path,[[->,'Symbol','Symbol','Bool']])
(: path 
  (-> Symbol Symbol Bool))


;; was base case, node to itself
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',=,[path,X,X],'True')
(= 
  (path $X $X) True)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',=,[path,X,Y],[and,[edge,X,Z],[path,Z,Y]])
(= 
  (path $X $Y) 
  (and 
    (edge $X $Z) 
    (path $Z $Y)))
